\int{{\frac{7 \, x^{2} + 18 \, x + 1}{4 \, x^{3} - 3 \, x^{2} + x}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{177}{28} \, \sqrt{7} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{7} {\left(8 \, x - 3\right)}\right) + \frac{3}{8} \, \log\left(4 \, x^{2} - 3 \, x + 1\right) + \log\left(x\right)}+C}

\end{problem}}%}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0061. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Compute the following integral:

\input{Integral-Compute-0061.HELP.tex}

\[
\int{{\frac{33 \, x^{2} + 33 \, x + 122}{7 \, x^{3} + 39 \, x^{2} - 10 \, x + 48}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{45}{301} \, \sqrt{215} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{215} \, \sqrt{215} {\left(14 \, x - 3\right)}\right) + \frac{5}{14} \, \log\left(7 \, x^{2} - 3 \, x + 8\right) + 4 \, \log\left(x + 6\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}
